We believe Windows Mixed Reality can be much more than that. We decided to design a casual game that people of all ages can play, share, and socialize in mixed reality. We were inspired by a classic interactive puzzle game for friends and family, while we were amazed by the potential of the mixed reality motion controllers, so Paint Arena was born. Many thanks to Mixed Reality Academy for the paint brush example.  \r\n\r\nInstructions:\r\nYou will need a HoloLens or a WMR immersive headset with a mixed reality motion controllers (and headphones, if not Samsung Odyssey) to enjoy this experience.\r\n\r\nThis social experience is best enjoyed in a casual standing pose. If you feel you are not at the right height after app launch, simply stand up, look forward, and say or tap \"Reset Floor Level\". \r\n\r\nYou could draw and talk to others and guess each others' drawings. If you are the first one to join, you would be assigned the drawer for the first round. You would be given a random word. Draw something to help others guess the word (without drawing any letters or digits). Once someone guesses your word correctly, a guesser will chosen at random to become the drawer. \r\n\r\nToggle \"Painting On\" to \"Paint Balling\" to start shooting paintballs and splatter the arena. Each full tank contains 100 paintballs. Every 5 seconds, you can partially refill the tank with 20 paintballs by pressing \"Refill 20 Paintballs\" button or saying the voice command \"Refill Paint Ball\". Try to move around to dodge incoming paintballs, or teleport to reposition. Score by reducing others' health bars to zero, upon which they would enter ghost mode and respawn at a random location in 10 seconds. \r\n\r\nIn Immersive headsets: Make sure you set up boundary for all experiences before you begin. While \"Painting On\", once you see your robotic right hand holding a paint brush, you can press the right hand trigger button to start drawing. While \"Paint Balling\", you can aim with your right hand controller, and press right hand trigger to shoot paintballs.\r\n\r\nOnce you see your robotic left arm holding a motion controller, you can use the touch pad to select paint color. Alternatively, you can tap \"Pick Color\" to bring up the large color wheel. \r\n\r\nIf you made a mistake, you can say \"Erase Last Stroke\" or press right hand controller grab button. You can also clear all strokes by saying \"Erase All Strokes\". \r\n\r\nTo rotate your view, point the joysticks left or right on one of the motion controllers. \r\n\r\nTo teleport, make sure the panel shows \"Teleport On\". Then point your cursor at the floor with one of the motion controllers, and hold the joystick forward until a Teleport marker appears, then release the joystick. \r\n\r\nIn HoloLens, you can use gaze, tap gesture to select options on the menu in front of you (look below chest level). You can use the same voice commands as elaborated above. While \"Painting On\", you can reach your hand out in front of you, pinch and hold while dragging the paint brush along. The game and its variants are popular in many countries and under various names.\r\n\r\nParchisi originated in India by the 6th century. \r\n\r\nEach player rolls the die; the highest roller begins the game. Once a player has one or more tokens in play, he selects a token and moves it forwards along the track the number of squares indicated by the dice. There are four players in two fixed partnerships. Partners sit facing each other. A standard 52 card pack is used. The cards in each suit rank from highest to lowest: A K Q J 10 9 8 7 6 5 4 3 2.\r\n\r\nThe player to the dealer's left leads to the first trick. Any card may be led. Den nederste del, der ikke brændes er sammensat af forskellige enheder, hvis det blandes farver - resterne af kastet former.\r\n\r\nDen anden tilstand er, når en faldende tal er sammensat af røde blokke, og de nederste blokke (lavet af de faldne dem) er blå.\r\n\r\nRetris giver en mulighed for at vise en transparent gitter, der opdeler et tal i blokke.\r\n\r\nSpillet kan vise en \"fantom\" - en identisk \"tvilling\" af et faldende tal til at hjælpe dig se, hvor det er bedre at placere den.\r\n\r\nMan kan vælge en tilstand af kontroltype i Quadris: Hvis du foretrækker at spille holde din smartphone eller tablet med to hænder, kan du vælge en tilstand, hvor betjeningsknapperne er beliggende til venstre og til højre fra spillet felt.\r\n\r\nDer er også en mulighed \"leg med den ene hånd\" i Quadris er betjeningsknapperne placeret til højre fra banen på din smartphone eller tablet-skærm.\r\n\r\nDu kan konkurrere med andre spillere som i mange andre puslespil. Efter at dine resultater komme ind i globale diagrammet.\r\n\r\nNyd den auto-save funktion, hvis dit spil bliver afbrudt af et opkald eller et andet program kontakten på smartphone!\r\n\r\nHvordan man spiller:\r\n- Opret vandrette linjer ved hjælp af faldende blokke;\r\n- Når du laver en linje af blokke, er det ryddet fra skærmen;\r\n- Spillet er slut, når blokkene hober sig op og nå toppen af ​​skærmen;\r\n- Du får flere point for at fuldføre flere linjer på en gang.\r\n\r\nDu kan spille den nye version af Quadris enten online og offline. Spillet kan være af interesse for både voksne fans af den klassiske Tetris spil og for at tiltrække den yngre generation, er det så nemt at bruge som pædagogiske onlinespil.\r\n\r\nFænomenet med klassiske puslespil - Tetris og andre relaterede puslespil spil som Quadris, Pentax, etc. - er gentagne gange blevet undersøgt af forskere. Hvis man tror deres mening, downloade et gratis puslespil (ligesom Quadris eller Tetris), får du både en fri krympning og en fri ernæringsekspert - det menes, at klassiske puslespil og logik spil kan lindre stress, kan bidrage til at lette sin tilstand efter psykologiske problemer og kan reducere risikoen for overspisning ved at skifte opmærksomhed til spillet.
